    const tagCount = () => {
        document.getElementById('qiitaTagCount').textContent = R.view(R.lensProp(document.getElementById('txt').value), qiitaTags)
        document.getElementById('teratailTagCount').textContent =　R.view(R.lensProp(document.getElementById('txt').value), teratailTags)
    }
    document.getElementById('txt').addEventListener('focus', tagCount, false);
    document.getElementById('txt').addEventListener('input', tagCount, false);

    const setTitleAndHref = (titleAndHref) => {
        let a = document.createElement('a'); a.textContent = titleAndHref[0]; a.href = titleAndHref[1];
        let li = document.createElement('li'); li.appendChild(a);
        let ul = document.getElementById('qiitaArticle'); ul.appendChild(li);
    }
    const getTitleAndHref = () => {
        fetch(`https://asia-northeast1-taro-fe94c.cloudfunctions.net/scrapingQiitaTagAndFeedJSONByJsdom?tag=${document.getElementById('txt').value}`).then(v => { return v.text() }).then(v => {

            R.forEach(setTitleAndHref, JSON.parse(v));
        })
    }
    document.getElementById('list').addEventListener('click', getTitleAndHref, false);

  <script>
    // 配列をシャッフルする関数
    const shuffleArray = array => {
      for (let i = array.length - 1; i > 0; i--) {
        let r = Math.floor(Math.random() * (i + 1));
        let tmp = array[i];
        array[i] = array[r];
        array[r] = tmp;
      }
      return array
    }

    // reference https://qiita.com/ttatsf/items/fdb9fc5dc12af7b6cb68
    // zip関数
    const zip = xs => ys =>
      (xs.length < ys.length) ? xs.map((e, i) => [e, ys[i]])
        : ys.map((e, i) => [xs[i], e]);

    // document.getElementById('foo').value =
    // "built\nbought\ncaught\ncut\nfelt\nfound";
    // "built\nbought\ncaught\ncut\nfelt\nfound\nhad\nheard\nkept\nleft\nlent";
    // "built\nbought\ncaught\ncut\nfelt\nfound\nhad\nheard\nkept\nleft\nlent\nlet\nlost\nmade\nmet\nput\nread\nsaid\nsold\nsent\nsat\nslept\nspent\nstood\ntaught\ntold\nthought\nunderstand";
    // document.getElementById('bar').value =
    // "建てた\n買った\n捕まった\nカット\nフェルト\n見つかった";
    // "建てた\n買った\n捕まった\nカット\nフェルト\n見つかった\n持っていました\n聞いた\n守った\n左\n貸した";
    // "建てた\n買った\n捕まった\nカット\nフェルト\n見つかった\n持っていました\n聞いた\n守った\n左\n貸した\nさせて\n迷った\n製\n会った\nプット\n読む\n前記\n売った\n送られた\n座っていた\n寝た\n費やした\n立っていた\n教えた\n言った\n思想\nわかる";

    // allShutudai:全部の出題
    let allShutudai = [];
    const makeAllShutudai = () => new Promise((resolve, reject) => {
      // 全問題から回答して減っていく問題の配列をコピー(参照渡しではないのでArray.from)
      let question = document.getElementById('foo').value.split('\n');
      let answer = document.getElementById('bar').value.split('\n');
      // mondai:全部の問題。破壊的変更はしない
      const mondai = zip(question)(answer);
      // shuffuledNokoriMondai:シャッフルしたあとの残りの全ての問題
      let shuffuledNokoriMondai = shuffleArray(Array.from(mondai))
      // 問題数分の出題を繰り返す
      const count = shuffuledNokoriMondai.length
      for (let i = 0; i < count; i++) {
        // seikai:正解の配列 1問分取り出す
        seikai = Array.from(shuffuledNokoriMondai.splice(0, 1))
        // shuffledMondai:全部の問題をシャッフルしたもの ランダムで正解とかぶってない配列だけを3つ取り出して不正解の配列を作る
        shuffledMondai = Array.from(shuffleArray(mondai))
        // fuseikai:不正解の配列
        fuseikai = Array.from(shuffledMondai.filter(v => v !== seikai[0]))
        // 全部の出題の配列にpushしていく
        allShutudai.push([fuseikai.splice(0, 3), seikai[0]])
      }
      resolve(allShutudai);
    })

    document.getElementById('btn').addEventListener('click', function () {
      makeAllShutudai().then(() => {
        init();
        keyConfig();
      }).catch((error) => {
        document.write(`失敗: ${error}`)
      })
    }, false);

    const init = () => {
      let score = document.createElement("a");
      score.setAttribute("id", "score");
      score.textContent = "0";
      document.querySelector("body").appendChild(score)

      let numberOfQuestions = document.createElement("a");
      numberOfQuestions.setAttribute("id", "numberOfQuestions");
      numberOfQuestions.textContent = `/${allShutudai.length}`;
      document.querySelector("body").appendChild(numberOfQuestions)

      for (let a of allShutudai) {
        let block = document.createElement("div");
        block.setAttribute("id", `mondaiBlock_${allShutudai.indexOf(a)}`);
        document.querySelector("body").appendChild(block)

        let text = document.createElement("text"); text.setAttribute("class", "question");
        text.textContent = `${a[1][0]}`;
        block.insertBefore(text, null)
        oneShutudai = shuffleArray(a[0].concat([[[a[1], "seikai"]]]));

        for (let i of oneShutudai) {
          // let div = document.createElement("div"); div.setAttribute("class", "bar"); block.insertBefore(div, null)

          let input = document.createElement("input");
          input.setAttribute("class", "question");
          input.setAttribute("type", "button");
          input.setAttribute("style", "width:100px;height:50px");
          if (i[0][1] === "seikai") {
            input.setAttribute("value", i[0][0][1]);
            input.setAttribute("name", i[0][1]);
          } else {
            input.setAttribute("value", i[1]);
          }
          block.appendChild(input);
        }
        let br = document.createElement("br"); block.insertBefore(br, null)
      }

      // let allButton = document.querySelectorAll('body > div > div > input');
      let allButton = document.querySelectorAll('body > div > input');
      allButton.forEach(button => {
        button.addEventListener('click', function () {
          if (button.name === "seikai") {
            // let mondaiBlock_Num = button.parentElement.parentElement.id;
            let mondaiBlock_Num = button.parentElement.id;
            document.getElementById(`${mondaiBlock_Num}`).parentNode.removeChild(document.getElementById(`${mondaiBlock_Num}`))
            score.textContent = (score.textContent - 0) + 1
          } else {
            console.log("fuseikai")
          };
        }, false);
      })
    }

    const keyConfig = () => {
      window.addEventListener("keydown", function (event) {
        if (event.defaultPrevented) {
          return; // Do nothing if the event was already processed
        }

        const choose = document.querySelector('body > div[id *= "mondaiBlock"]');

        switch (event.key) {
          case "Down": // IE/Edge specific value
          case "ArrowDown":
            // Do something for "down arrow" key press.
            choose.querySelectorAll('input').item(2).click()
            break;
          case "Up": // IE/Edge specific value
          case "ArrowUp":
            // Do something for "up arrow" key press.
            choose.querySelectorAll('input').item(1).click()
            break;
          case "Left": // IE/Edge specific value
          case "ArrowLeft":
            // Do something for "left arrow" key press.
            choose.querySelectorAll('input').item(0).click()
          // mondai.querySelectorAll('input').item(0).addEventListener("keydown", function (event) { console.log("hogehoge") })            break;
          case "Right": // IE/Edge specific value
          case "ArrowRight":
            // Do something for "right arrow" key press.
            choose.querySelectorAll('input').item(3).click()
            break;
          // case "Enter":
          //   // Do something for "enter" or "return" key press.
          //   break;
          // case "Esc": // IE/Edge specific value
          // case "Escape":
          //   // Do something for "esc" key press.
          //   break;
          default:
          // return; // Quit when this doesn't handle the key event.
        }

        // Cancel the default action to avoid it being handled twice
        event.preventDefault();
      }, true);
    }

  </script>

  <script>
    let res = [];
    let joinedRes = [];

    document.getElementById('btn').addEventListener('click', function () {
      let bar = document.getElementById('foo').value.split('');

      while (bar.length !== 0) { if (bar.length === 0) { break } res.push(bar.splice(0, 110)) }
      res.map(v => joinedRes.push(v.join('')))

      for (let dataText of joinedRes) {
        let a = document.createElement("a"); a.setAttribute("class", "twitter-share-button"); a.setAttribute("data-text", dataText);
        let script = document.createElement("script"); script.setAttribute("src", "https://platform.twitter.com/widgets.js"); script.setAttribute("charset", "utf-8");
        document.querySelector("body").insertBefore(a, null)
        document.querySelector("body").insertBefore(script, null)
      }
    }, false);
  </script>

    let test = false;
     function testExe() {
        test = await true;
        await document.querySelector("#button1").click();
        document.form1.text1.value = await "abc";
        await document.querySelector("#button1").click();
        await document.querySelector("#deleteAll").click();
    }

    // store resource from "chache"
    function cacheOn() {
        firebase.firestore().enablePersistence({
            synchronizeTabs: true
        })
        storeResource = {
            source: "cache"
        };
    }

    function create() {
        firebase.firestore().collection("users").add({
            foo: "bar",
            foo2: "bar2"
        }).then(docRef => {
            if (test === false) {
                db(); //
            }
            console.log("Document written with ID: ", docRef.id);
        }).catch(error => {
            console.error("Error adding document: ", error);
        });
    }

    function createText() {
        document.form1.text1.value === "" ? text = "test" : text = document.form1.text1.value;
        firebase.firestore().collection("users").add({
            foo: "bar",
            // foo2: `${document.form1.text1.value}`
            foo2: `${text}`
        }).then(docRef => {
            console.log("Document written with ID: ", docRef.id);
        }).then(() => {
            if (test === false) {
                db(); //
            }
        }).catch(error => {
            console.error("Error adding document: ", error);
        });
    }

    // DOM append
    function append(text, id) {
        let div = document.createElement('div');
        div.textContent = text;
        div.setAttribute("id", id);
        document.querySelector('#result').appendChild(div);
    }

    function read() {
        firebase.firestore().collection("users").get(
            storeResource
        ).then(col => {
            col.forEach(doc => {
                console.log(`${doc.id} => ${doc.data().foo2}`);
                append(`${doc.data().foo2}`, doc.id);
            });
        })
    }

    // READ collection, document, field, append Delete function to div elements
    function readAndAppendDelete() {
        // remove element before rendering
        let element = document.querySelector("#result");
        while (element.firstChild) element.removeChild(element.firstChild);

        firebase.firestore().collection("users").get(
            storeResource
        ).then(col => {
            col.forEach(doc => {
                console.log(`${doc.id} => ${doc.data().foo2}`);
                append(`${doc.data().foo2}`, doc.id);
            });
        }).then(() => {
            // append Delete function to div elements
            document.querySelectorAll("div").forEach(e => {
                e.addEventListener("click", deleteDocument, false)
            });
        })
    }

    function update() {
        firebase.firestore().collection("users").doc("DYDZjsIUFYxPvi5QTARH").update({
            foo2: "hogehoge"
        }).then(() => {
            console.dir("UPDATE SUCCESS");
        });
    }

    function deleteDocument(e) {
        firebase.firestore().collection("users").doc(e.target.id).delete().then((result) => {
            console.dir("SUCCESS")
        }).then(function () {
            if (test === false) {
                db(); //
            }
        }).catch(function (error) {
            console.error("ERROR: ", error);
        });
    }

    function deleteField() {
        firebase.firestore().collection("users").doc("2").update({
            foo: firebase.firestore.FieldValue.delete()
        });
    }

    function deleteAllDocuments() {
        firebase.firestore().collection("users").get().then(col => {
            col.forEach(doc => {
                firebase.firestore().collection("users").doc(
                    `${doc.id}`
                ).delete().then((result) => {
                    console.dir("SUCCESS");
                    if (test === false) {
                        db(); //
                    }
                }).catch(function (error) {
                    console.error("ERROR: ", error);
                });
            });
        });
        // DELETE collection is no API, use DELETE each document
    }


     function db() {

    document.addEventListener('DOMContentLoaded', db, false);

	const addWikiHTML = (array) =>{
		const innerArraySetForMakeHTML = (innerArray,KEY) => {
			return `<div class="searchResult" data-id="${KEY}">${innerArray.snippet}</div>`;
		}
		document.querySelector(`#result`).insertAdjacentHTML(`afterBegin`,  array.map(innerArraySetForMakeHTML).join('') );
	};
	const getWikiText = (endpoint) =>{
		// fetch(`https://ja.wikipedia.org/w/api.php?action=query&list=search&prop=info&inprop=url&utf8=&format=json&origin=*&srlimit=3&srsearch=tokyo`).then(
		fetch(endpoint).then(v=>{
			return v.text()
		}).then(v => { 
			addWikiHTML(JSON.parse(v).query.search);
		}).then(v=>{
			document.querySelector("textarea").value = document.querySelector("#result").textContent;
			count();
		});
	}
	function handleSubmit(event) {
		event.preventDefault();

		const searchQuery = input.trim();
		fetchResults(searchQuery);
	}
	function fetchResults(searchQuery) {
		const endpoint = `https://en.wikipedia.org/w/api.php?action=query&list=search&prop=info&inprop=url&utf8=&format=json&origin=*&srlimit=3&srsearch=${searchQuery}`;
		getWikiText(endpoint);
	}

const movePositionLeft = (howLongMovePosition) => {
	try{if(0 > textPosition){throw new Error()}
		document.querySelector('#textField').focus();
		textPosition<0 ? textPosition=0 : textPosition-=howLongMovePosition;
		document.querySelector('#textField').setSelectionRange(textPosition,textPosition);
	}catch(e){}
}
const movePositionRight = (howLongMovePosition) => {
	try{if(document.querySelector('#textField').value.length < textPosition){throw new Error()}
		document.querySelector('#textField').focus();
		textPosition<0 ? textPosition=0 : textPosition+=howLongMovePosition;
		document.querySelector('#textField').setSelectionRange(textPosition,textPosition);
	}catch(e){}
}

const shuffleArray = array => {
	for (let i = array.length - 1; i > 0; i--) {
	let r = Math.floor(Math.random() * (i + 1));
	let tmp = array[i];
	array[i] = array[r];
	array[r] = tmp;
	}
	return array
}

const keyConfig = () => {
	window.addEventListener("keydown", function (event) {
	if (event.defaultPrevented) {
		return; // Do nothing if the event was already processed
	}
		switch (event.key) {
		case "1":
			document.querySelectorAll('div.QA > input').item(0).click()
		break;
		case "2":
			document.querySelectorAll('div.QA > input').item(1).click()
		break;
		case "3":
			document.querySelectorAll('div.QA > input').item(2).click()
		break;
		case "4":
			document.querySelectorAll('div.QA > input').item(3).click()
		break;
		case "Enter":
		default:
		}
	// Cancel the default action to avoid it being handled twice
	event.preventDefault();
	}, true);
}

let reverse;
let shuffle;
const insertData = () =>{
	document.querySelectorAll("#QASet > div").forEach(E=>{E.parentNode.removeChild(E)});
	const overTwoElementArray = R.filter(n => n.length > 1, allfunctions);
	const withoutZeroElmArray = R.map(R.drop(1), overTwoElementArray);
	const onlyZeroElmArray = R.pipe(R.map(R.take(1)), R.unnest)(overTwoElementArray);
	const withoutZeroElmArrayJoined = R.map(V => R.join(" ")(V), withoutZeroElmArray)
	let onlyZeroElmArrayAndWithoutZeroElmArrayJoined = R.pipe(
		R.transpose,
	)([	onlyZeroElmArray, withoutZeroElmArrayJoined ]);
	onlyZeroElmArrayAndWithoutZeroElmArrayJoined = reverse === 1 ? R.reverse(onlyZeroElmArrayAndWithoutZeroElmArrayJoined) : onlyZeroElmArrayAndWithoutZeroElmArrayJoined;
	onlyZeroElmArrayAndWithoutZeroElmArrayJoined = shuffle === 1 ? shuffleArray(onlyZeroElmArrayAndWithoutZeroElmArrayJoined) : onlyZeroElmArrayAndWithoutZeroElmArrayJoined;
	const [foo, bar] = [R.pluck(0, onlyZeroElmArrayAndWithoutZeroElmArrayJoined).join("\n"), R.pluck(1, onlyZeroElmArrayAndWithoutZeroElmArrayJoined).join("\n") ];
	document.querySelector(`#foo`).value = foo;
	document.querySelector(`#bar`).value = bar;
};

const makeQApair = () => R.transpose([ document.querySelector(`#foo`).value.split(`\n`) , document.querySelector(`#bar`).value.split(`\n`) ]) ;

const getQAAAAarray = (QApair) => {
	const makeQAAAAarray = (x) => R.insertAll(-1,
											  R.take(3,
											  		shuffleArray(
														R.without(x[1],
																  R.pluck(1, QApair)))),
											  x);
	const fourLengthArrayCheck = (array) => R.uniq(array).length < 4;
	return R.reject( fourLengthArrayCheck ,  R.map(makeQAAAAarray, QApair)  );
};

		return `<div class="QA" data-id="${KEY}">
					<span onclick="show('${QAAAA[0]}')">${QAAAA[0]}</span>
					<input type="button" value="${shuffledAAAA[0]}" data-answer="${QAAAA[1]}" data-id="${KEY}" onclick="checkQA(event)"></input>
					<input type="button" value="${shuffledAAAA[1]}" data-answer="${QAAAA[1]}" data-id="${KEY}" onclick="checkQA(event)"></input>
					<input type="button" value="${shuffledAAAA[2]}" data-answer="${QAAAA[1]}" data-id="${KEY}" onclick="checkQA(event)"></input>
					<input type="button" value="${shuffledAAAA[3]}" data-answer="${QAAAA[1]}" data-id="${KEY}" onclick="checkQA(event)"></input>
					${referenceFunction.join("")}
			   </div>`;
	}
	document.querySelector(`#QASet`).insertAdjacentHTML(`afterBegin`,  QAAAAarray.map(makeQASet).join("") );
};

<script>
const shuffleArray = array => {
	for (let i = array.length - 1; i > 0; i--) {
	let r = Math.floor(Math.random() * (i + 1));
	let tmp = array[i];
	array[i] = array[r];
	array[r] = tmp;
	}
	return array
}

const keyConfig = () => {
	window.addEventListener("keydown", function (event) {
	if (event.defaultPrevented) {
		return; // Do nothing if the event was already processed
	}
		switch (event.key) {
		case "1":
			document.querySelectorAll('div.QA > input').item(0).click()
		break;
		case "2":
			document.querySelectorAll('div.QA > input').item(1).click()
		break;
		case "3":
			document.querySelectorAll('div.QA > input').item(2).click()
		break;
		case "4":
			document.querySelectorAll('div.QA > input').item(3).click()
		break;
		case "Enter":
		default:
		}
	// Cancel the default action to avoid it being handled twice
	event.preventDefault();
	}, true);
}

let reverse;
let shuffle;
let ramdajsfunctionmaskqa;
// const functionNameAndSampleCode from ./functionNameAndSampleCode.js
const makeRamdajsfunctionmaskqa = ()=>{
	return functionNameAndSampleCode.map(VAL => {
		const functionName = R.pluck(0,functionNameAndSampleCode);
		const otherFunctionName = R.without(VAL[0], functionName);
		const shuffleOtherFunctionName = shuffleArray(otherFunctionName);
		const shuffleOtherFunctionNameThree = R.take(3,shuffleOtherFunctionName);
		const AAAA = R.prepend(VAL[0], shuffleOtherFunctionNameThree);
		const shuffledAAAA = shuffleArray(AAAA);
		const QshuffledAAAA = R.prepend(VAL[0], shuffledAAAA);
		return QshuffledAAAA
	})
}

const makeQAHTML = (QAAAAarray) =>{
	const makeQASet = (QAAAA,KEY) => {
		const AAAA = R.takeLast(4,QAAAA);
		const referenceFunction = R.pipe(R.split(" "),R.map(V=>{return `<span onclick="show('${V}')">${V} </span>`}))(AAAA[0]+` `+AAAA[1]+` `+AAAA[2]+` `+AAAA[3]);
		const answerText = document.querySelector(`#${QAAAA[0]} + section`).querySelector(".javascript").innerText;
		const maskAnswerText = answerText.replace(new RegExp(QAAAA[0], 'g'), "~");
		return `<div class="QA" data-id="${KEY}">
						<span onclick="show('${QAAAA[0]}')">${maskAnswerText}</span>
						<input type="button" value="${AAAA[0]}" data-answer="${QAAAA[0]}" data-id="${KEY}" onclick="checkQA(event)"></input>
						<input type="button" value="${AAAA[1]}" data-answer="${QAAAA[0]}" data-id="${KEY}" onclick="checkQA(event)"></input>
						<input type="button" value="${AAAA[2]}" data-answer="${QAAAA[0]}" data-id="${KEY}" onclick="checkQA(event)"></input>
						<input type="button" value="${AAAA[3]}" data-answer="${QAAAA[0]}" data-id="${KEY}" onclick="checkQA(event)"></input>
						${referenceFunction.join("")}
				</div>`;
	}
	document.querySelector(`#QASet`).insertAdjacentHTML(`afterBegin`,  QAAAAarray.map(makeQASet).join("") );
};

let wrongQApair = [];
const checkWorkOut = () =>{ if(document.querySelector(`#point`).innerText === document.querySelector(`#allPoint`).innerText){ TIMER.stop() } };
const checkQA = (event) =>{
							if(event.target.value === event.target.dataset.answer){
								document.querySelector(`div.QA[data-id="${event.target.dataset.id}"`).parentNode.removeChild( document.querySelector(`div.QA[data-id="${event.target.dataset.id}"`) )
							// }else{ wrongQApair.push( [ QAAAAarray[event.target.dataset.id][0], QAAAAarray[event.target.dataset.id][1] ] ) };
							}
							countPoint();
							checkWorkOut();
							localStorage.saveData = document.querySelector("body").outerHTML;
						  };

	document.querySelector(`body`).insertAdjacentHTML(`beforeend`, htmlstring);
};

const show = (functionName) =>{
	document.querySelectorAll("body div#QASet code").forEach(E=>{E.parentNode.removeChild(E)});
	document.querySelector(`body div#QASet`).insertAdjacentHTML(`afterbegin`, document.querySelector(`#${functionName} + section`).querySelector(".javascript").outerHTML);
	document.querySelector(`body div#QASet code`).addEventListener("click", () => document.querySelectorAll("body div#QASet code").forEach(E=>{E.parentNode.removeChild(E)}));
}

const countPoint = () => document.querySelector(`#point`).innerText = Number(document.querySelector(`#allPoint`).innerText) - document.querySelectorAll(`#QASet > div`).length;

	document.querySelectorAll(".QA").forEach(E=>{E.parentNode.removeChild(E)});
	ramdajsfunctionmaskqa = makeRamdajsfunctionmaskqa();
	ramdajsfunctionmaskqa = reverse === 1 ? R.reverse(ramdajsfunctionmaskqa) : ramdajsfunctionmaskqa;
	ramdajsfunctionmaskqa = shuffle === 1 ? shuffleArray(ramdajsfunctionmaskqa) : ramdajsfunctionmaskqa;
	makeQAHTML( ramdajsfunctionmaskqa );

}

<script>
const shuffleArray = array => {
	for (let i = array.length - 1; i > 0; i--) {
	let r = Math.floor(Math.random() * (i + 1));
	let tmp = array[i];
	array[i] = array[r];
	array[r] = tmp;
	}
	return array
}

const keyConfig = () => {
	window.addEventListener("keydown", function (event) {
	if (event.defaultPrevented) {
		return; // Do nothing if the event was already processed
	}
		switch (event.key) {
		case "1":
			document.querySelectorAll('div.QA > input').item(0).click()
		break;
		case "2":
			document.querySelectorAll('div.QA > input').item(1).click()
		break;
		case "3":
			document.querySelectorAll('div.QA > input').item(2).click()
		break;
		case "4":
			document.querySelectorAll('div.QA > input').item(3).click()
		break;
		case "Enter":
		default:
		}
	// Cancel the default action to avoid it being handled twice
	event.preventDefault();
	}, true);
}

let reverse;
let shuffle;
let ramdajsfunctionmaskqa;

const makeRamdajsfunctionmaskqa = ()=>{
	const question = Array.from(document.querySelectorAll(`.javascript`)).map(V=>R.replace(/\/\/=>.*/gi,"~",  V.innerText ));
	const answer = Array.from(document.querySelectorAll(`.javascript`)).map(V=>R.replace(/["'`]/g,"",R.join("")(R.match(/\/\/=>.*/gi, V.innerText))));
	const AWithshuffledAAAAarray = answer.map(V=>{
		const shuffledOtherAnswer = shuffleArray(R.without([V], answer));
		const shuffledOtherAnswerThree = R.take(3,shuffledOtherAnswer);
		const shuffledAAAAarray = shuffleArray(R.prepend(V, shuffledOtherAnswerThree));
		const AWithshuffledAAAAarray = R.prepend(V, shuffledAAAAarray);
		return	AWithshuffledAAAAarray;
	})
	const QAWithshuffledAAAAarray = R.transpose([question,AWithshuffledAAAAarray]);
	const QAWithshuffledFlattedAAAAarray = R.map(R.flatten)(QAWithshuffledAAAAarray);
	const filteredQAWithshuffledAAAAarray = R.filter(V => { if( R.not( R.isEmpty(V[1])) ){ return V } }, QAWithshuffledFlattedAAAAarray);
	console.log(filteredQAWithshuffledAAAAarray);
	return filteredQAWithshuffledAAAAarray;
}

const makeQAHTML = (filteredQAWithshuffledAAAAarray) =>{
	const makeQASet = (QAWithAAAA,KEY) => {
		const AAAA = R.takeLast(4,QAWithAAAA);
						// <span onclick="show('${QAWithAAAA[0]}')">${QAWithAAAA[0]}</span>
		return `<div class="QA" data-id="${KEY}">
						<span>${QAWithAAAA[0]}</span>
						<input type="button" value='${AAAA[0]}' data-answer="${QAWithAAAA[1]}" data-id="${KEY}" onclick="checkQA(event)"></input>
						<input type="button" value='${AAAA[1]}' data-answer="${QAWithAAAA[1]}" data-id="${KEY}" onclick="checkQA(event)"></input>
						<input type="button" value='${AAAA[2]}' data-answer="${QAWithAAAA[1]}" data-id="${KEY}" onclick="checkQA(event)"></input>
						<input type="button" value='${AAAA[3]}' data-answer="${QAWithAAAA[1]}" data-id="${KEY}" onclick="checkQA(event)"></input>
				</div>`;
	}
	document.querySelector(`#QASet`).insertAdjacentHTML(`afterBegin`,  filteredQAWithshuffledAAAAarray.map(makeQASet).join("") );
};

let wrongQApair = [];

							// }else{ wrongQApair.push( [ QAAAAarray[event.target.dataset.id][0], QAAAAarray[event.target.dataset.id][1] ] ) };

let data, infoWindow;
function initMap(){
	data = new google.maps.Map(document.getElementById('map'), {
		center: {lat:mapData[0][1],lng:mapData[0][2]},
		zoom: 14
   });
   infoWindow = new google.maps.InfoWindow;

	// HTML5 geolocation.
	if (navigator.geolocation) {
		navigator.geolocation.getCurrentPosition(function(position) {
		const pos = {
			lat: position.coords.latitude,
			lng: position.coords.longitude
		};

		infoWindow.setPosition(pos);
		infoWindow.setContent('Location found.');
		infoWindow.open(data);
		data.setCenter(pos);
		}, function() {
		handleLocationError(true, infoWindow, data.getCenter());
		});
	} else {
		// Browser doesn't support Geolocation
		handleLocationError(false, infoWindow, data.getCenter());
	}

	let marker = [];
	mapData.map((VAL,KEY)=>{
		marker[KEY] = new google.maps.Marker({
			position: {lat: VAL[1], lng: VAL[2]},
			map: data,
			title: VAL[0]
		});
	})
};

function handleLocationError(browserHasGeolocation, infoWindow, pos) {
	infoWindow.setPosition(pos);
	infoWindow.setContent(browserHasGeolocation ?
							'Error: The Geolocation service failed.' :
							'Error: Your browser doesn\'t support geolocation.');
	infoWindow.open(map);
}
</script>

<script>
const TIMER = new easytimer.Timer();
TIMER.addEventListener('targetAchieved', () => document.querySelector('.RESULT').innerText = "TIME IS COMING!!" );
// TIMER.addEventListener('secondsUpdated', () => document.querySelector('.RESULT').innerText = TIMER.getTimeValues().toString() );
TIMER.addEventListener('secondTenthsUpdated', () => document.querySelector('.RESULT').innerText = TIMER.getTimeValues().toString(['hours', 'minutes', 'seconds', 'secondTenths']) );
// TIMER.addEventListener('secondTenthsUpdated', () => document.querySelector('.RESULT').innerText = TIMER.getTimeValues().toString(['minutes']) );
let [HH, MM, SS] = ["","",""];
let STARTED;

//   if(localStorage.saveData){document.querySelector(`#TIMEINPUT`).value = JSON.parse(localStorage.saveData)};
const TIMEINPUT=()=>{
  [HH, MM, SS] = (document.querySelector(`#TIMEINPUT`).value).split(':');
  if(!HH)HH='00';if(!MM)MM='00';if(!SS)SS='00';
  if(document.querySelector(`#TIMEINPUT`).value === "" || document.querySelector(`#TIMEINPUT`).value === "00:00"){ document.querySelector(`#TIMEINPUT`).value = "00:00:00" };
//   document.querySelector('#INJAPANESE').innerText = `${HH}時${MM}分${SS}秒`;
  if(STARTED){TIMER.stop();STARTED=false};
//   localStorage.saveData = JSON.stringify(document.querySelector(`#TIMEINPUT`).value);
}

const USETIMER=()=>{
	STARTED=true;
	SS = Number(SS) + Number(MM)*60 + Number(HH)*3600;
	// TIMER.start({ countdown: true, startValues: {seconds: Number(SS)}, target: { seconds: 0 } });
	TIMER.start({ countdown: true, startValues: {seconds: Number(SS)}, target: { seconds: 0 }, precision: 'secondTenths' });
	// document.querySelector('.RESULT').innerText = TIMER.getTimeValues().toString();
	document.querySelector('.RESULT').innerText = TIMER.getTimeValues().toString(['hours', 'minutes', 'seconds', 'secondTenths']);
}
const TIMERPAUSE=()=>TIMER.pause();
const TIMERSTOP=()=>TIMER.stop();
const TIMERRESET=()=>TIMER.reset();
// const RESUME=()=>TIMER.start({ countdown: true, startValues: {seconds: SS}, target: { seconds: 0 } });
const RESUME=()=>TIMER.start({ countdown: true, startValues: {seconds: SS}, target: { seconds: 0 }, precision: 'secondTenths' });


const makeEditableButtonListArrayIndexList = (fooArray) => {
	document.querySelectorAll(".timerArrayItem").forEach(E=>{E.parentNode.removeChild(E)});
	const makeEditableButtonListArrayIndexListHTMLStr = (ELEMENT,KEY) => `<button class="timerArrayItem" data-idx="${KEY}" onclick="insertTimer(event);">${KEY}</button>`;
	document.querySelector(`#timerArray`).insertAdjacentHTML(`beforeEnd`,  fooArray.map(makeEditableButtonListArrayIndexListHTMLStr).join("")  );
};
const insertTimer = (idx) =>{
	document.querySelector(`#TIMEINPUT`).value = JSON.parse(localStorage.saveData)[Number(event.target.dataset.idx)];
	TIMEINPUT();
};

let timerArray=[];
const saveTimerArray = () =>{
	timerArray.push(document.querySelector(`#TIMEINPUT`).value);
	localStorage.saveData = JSON.stringify( timerArray  );
	makeEditableButtonListArrayIndexList(timerArray);
};
const loadTimerArray = () =>{
	timerArray = JSON.parse(localStorage.saveData);
	makeEditableButtonListArrayIndexList(timerArray);
};
const clearTimerSaveData = () =>{
	localStorage.clear();
	timerArray=[];
	document.querySelectorAll(".timerArrayItem").forEach(E=>{E.parentNode.removeChild(E)});
};

<script>
let NEWTIMERARRAY=[];
const NEWTIMER = ()=>{
	NEWTIMERARRAY = R.range(0, document.querySelectorAll(".TIMEINPUTS").length + 1);
	document.querySelectorAll(".TIMEINPUTS").forEach(E=>{E.parentNode.removeChild(E)});
	const makeEditableButtonListArrayIndexListHTMLStr = (ELEMENT,KEY) => `<input class="TIMEINPUTS" type="time" value="00:00:00" data-timeridx=${KEY} step="1" oninput="TIMEINPUT();">`;
	document.querySelector(`#ALLTIMER`).insertAdjacentHTML(`beforeEnd`,  NEWTIMERARRAY.map(makeEditableButtonListArrayIndexListHTMLStr).join("")  );
}

let TIMER = new easytimer.Timer();
TIMER.addEventListener('secondTenthsUpdated', () => document.querySelector('.RESULT').innerText = TIMER.getTimeValues().toString(['hours', 'minutes', 'seconds', 'secondTenths']) );
document.querySelector('.RESULT').innerText = TIMER.getTimeValues().toString(['hours', 'minutes', 'seconds', 'secondTenths']);

let ALLTIMER = [];
let CURRENTTIMER;
TIMER.addEventListener('targetAchieved', () => {
	if(R.isEmpty(ALLTIMER)){
		document.querySelector('.RESULT').innerText = "TIME IS COMING!!"}
	else{
		CURRENTTIMER = R.head(ALLTIMER);
		ALLTIMER = R.remove(0, 1, ALLTIMER);
		TIMER.start({ countdown: true, startValues: {seconds: Number(CURRENTTIMER)}, target: { seconds: 0 }, precision: 'secondTenths' });
	}
});

let [HH, MM, SS] = ["","",""];

const TIMEINPUT=()=>{
	ALLTIMER=[];
	document.querySelectorAll(".TIMEINPUTS").forEach(V=>{
		[HH, MM, SS] = (V.value).split(':');
		if(!HH)HH='00';if(!MM)MM='00';if(!SS)SS='00';
		if(V.value === "" || V.value === "00:00"){ V.value = "00:00:00" };
		ALLTIMER.push(Number(SS) + Number(MM)*60 + Number(HH)*3600);
	})
}

const USETIMER=()=>{
	CURRENTTIMER = R.head(ALLTIMER);
	ALLTIMER = R.remove(0, 1, ALLTIMER);
	TIMER.start({ countdown: true, startValues: {seconds: Number(CURRENTTIMER)}, target: { seconds: 0 }, precision: 'secondTenths' });
}
const TIMERPAUSE=()=>TIMER.pause();
const TIMERSTOP=()=>TIMER.stop();
const TIMERRESET=()=>TIMER.reset();
const RESUME=()=>TIMER.start({ countdown: true, startValues: {seconds: SS}, target: { seconds: 0 }, precision: 'secondTenths' });

let SAVETIMERARRAY=[];
const SAVESAVETIMERARRAY = () =>{
	document.querySelectorAll(`.TIMEINPUTS`).forEach(V=>{SAVETIMERARRAY.push(V.value)});
	localStorage.saveData = JSON.stringify( SAVETIMERARRAY );
};
const LOADSAVETIMERARRAY = () =>{
	document.querySelectorAll(".TIMEINPUTS").forEach(E=>{E.parentNode.removeChild(E)});
	SAVETIMERARRAY = JSON.parse(localStorage.saveData);
	const MAKETIMER = (VAL,KEY) => `<input class="TIMEINPUTS" type="time" value=${VAL} data-timeridx=${KEY} step="1" oninput="TIMEINPUT();">`;
	document.querySelector(`#ALLTIMER`).insertAdjacentHTML(`beforeEnd`,  SAVETIMERARRAY.map(MAKETIMER).join("")  );
};
const CLEARTIMERSAVEDATA = () =>{
	localStorage.clear();
	document.querySelectorAll(".TIMEINPUTS").forEach(E=>{E.parentNode.removeChild(E)});
	ALLSAVETIMERARRAY=[0];
};

<a target="_blank" rel="noopener noreferrer" href="https://script.google.com/macros/s/AKfycbyhMMEzWxNMmxZzyn8f9ot2YdROT9UThZeba_an3YDun2F0hot2/exec?value=foo" onclick="textShare()">Share</a>

<script>
new ClipboardJS('.btn');

const textShare = () =>{
	const query = encodeURIComponent(document.querySelector(`#textField`).value);
	const URL = document.querySelector("a").href = "https://script.google.com/macros/s/AKfycbyhMMEzWxNMmxZzyn8f9ot2YdROT9UThZeba_an3YDun2F0hot2/exec?value=" + query;
	// console.log(URL);

	// long URL, it cant make unreadable QRCode by phone camera
	// new QRCode(document.querySelector("#qrcode"), URL);

	// make bitly URL, that response JSON with shorter URL and make QRCode by shorter URL
	// fetch('http://example.com/movies.json')
	fetch(`https://api-ssl.bitly.com/v3/shorten?access_token=68c5b0fd0c41d25ab07ee7d7945242daf0fd5091&longUrl=${encodeURIComponent(URL)}`)
	.then((response) => {
		return response.json();
	})
	.then((json) => {
		// console.log(json.data.url);
		new QRCode(document.querySelector("#qrcode"), json.data.url);
		document.querySelector(`body`).insertAdjacentHTML(`afterBegin`, 
			`<textarea name="url" id="url" cols="20" rows="1">${json.data.url}</textarea>
			<button class="btn" data-clipboard-target="#url">COPY URL</button>` 
		);
	});
}

<script>
	// all of global values
	// saveDataArray is	[allBlockNum, blockVolume, madeDate, editedDate] => [allBlockNum, Number(document.querySelector("#number1").value), moment().format(), moment().format()]
	let saveDataArray=[];
	let allBlockNum=0;
	let editElmNum;
	
	// utility functions
	const debug = () =>{
		console.table(
			localStorage.saveData
		);
	}

	const test = () =>{
		localStorage.clear();
		document.querySelector("#number1").value = 1;
		document.querySelector(`#add`).click();
		document.querySelector(`#add`).click();
		document.querySelector(`#add`).click();
		document.querySelector(`#reduce`).click();
		document.querySelector(`#addSaveData`).click();

		document.querySelector("#number1").value = 3;
		document.querySelector(`#add`).click();
		document.querySelector(`#add`).click();
		document.querySelector(`#add`).click();
		document.querySelector(`#reduce`).click();
		document.querySelector(`#addSaveData`).click();
		document.querySelector(`#deleteAllBlock`).click();
	}

	// make block functions
	const addHTML = (array) =>{
		const innerArraySetForMakeHTML = (innerArray,KEY) => {
			return `<li class="block" data-id="${KEY}">${innerArray[1]}</li>`;
		}
		document.querySelector(`#htmlblocks`).insertAdjacentHTML(`afterBegin`, array.map(innerArraySetForMakeHTML).join(''));
		debug();
	};

	const ifEdit = () =>{
		if(editElmNum){
			saveDataArray[editElmNum][0] = allBlockNum;
			saveDataArray[editElmNum][1] = Number(document.querySelector("#number1").value);
			// saveDataArray[editElmNum][2] is madeDate
			saveDataArray[editElmNum][3] = moment().format();
			localStorage.saveData = JSON.stringify(saveDataArray);
			deleteAllSaveDataHTML();
			addSaveDataHTML( saveDataArray );
		}
	}

	const makeBlock = () =>{
		document.querySelectorAll("li.block").forEach(E=>{E.parentNode.removeChild(E)});
		addHTML(R.transpose( [ R.times(R.identity, allBlockNum), R.repeat('▨', allBlockNum) ] ));
	}

	const addBlock = () =>{
		document.querySelector("#allBlockNum").innerText = allBlockNum +=
		Number(document.querySelector("#number1").value);
		ifEdit();
		makeBlock();
	}

	const reduceBlock = () =>{
		document.querySelector("#allBlockNum").innerText = allBlockNum -=
		Number(document.querySelector("#number1").value);
		ifEdit();
		makeBlock();
	};

	const deleteAllBlock = () =>{
		document.querySelector("#allBlockNum").innerText = allBlockNum = 0;
		ifEdit();
		makeBlock();
	}

	// save/load functions	
	const addSaveDataHTML = (array) =>{
		const innerArraySetForMakeHTML = (innerArray,KEY) => {
			return `<li onclick="setSaveDataFunc(event)" class="savedata" data-save-id="${KEY}" data-all-block-num-list="${innerArray[0]}"
					data-blocks-num-list="${innerArray[1]}" style="padding: 1px 10px;background: #5876a3; pointer-events: auto;">
					<span class="allBlockNumList" style="pointer-events: none;">${innerArray[0]}</span>
					<span class="blocksNumList" style="pointer-events: none;">${innerArray[1]}</span>
					</li><li class="list2" data-foo="${KEY}" style="padding: 1px 10px;background: purple;" onclick="deleteSaveDataFunc(event)">delete button</li>`;
		}
		document.querySelector(`#savedatas`).insertAdjacentHTML(`afterBegin`, array.map(innerArraySetForMakeHTML).join(''));
	};

	const deleteAllSaveDataHTML = () =>{
		document.querySelectorAll("li.savedata").forEach(E=>{E.parentNode.removeChild(E)});
		document.querySelectorAll("li.list2").forEach(E=>{E.parentNode.removeChild(E)});
	}

	const loadSaveDataFunc = () => {
		saveDataArray = JSON.parse(localStorage.saveData);
		deleteAllSaveDataHTML();
		addSaveDataHTML(saveDataArray);
	}

	const addSaveDataFunc = () => {
		saveDataArray.push( [allBlockNum, Number(document.querySelector("#number1").value), moment().format(), moment().format()] );
		// saveDataArray.push( [allBlockNum, Number(document.querySelector("#number1").value)] );
		localStorage.saveData = JSON.stringify(saveDataArray);
		loadSaveDataFunc();
	};

	const setSaveDataFunc = (event) => {
		editElmNum = event.target.dataset.saveId;
		// Implicit conversion Number to String
		document.querySelector("#allBlockNum").innerText = allBlockNum = Number(event.target.dataset.allBlockNumList);
		document.querySelector("#number1").value = event.target.dataset.blocksNumList;
		makeBlock();
		debug();
	}

	const deleteSaveDataFunc = (event) => {
		// destructive function: splice()
		saveDataArray.splice(Number(event.target.dataset.foo), 1);
		localStorage.saveData = JSON.stringify(saveDataArray);
		deleteAllSaveDataHTML();
		addSaveDataHTML( saveDataArray );
	}

	test();
	loadSaveDataFunc();

	const earlyVal = moment();
	console.log(earlyVal);
	const lateVal = moment();
	console.log(lateVal);
	console.log(`lateVal defined late ${lateVal.diff(earlyVal)} milliseconds from earlyVal`);
	if(lateVal>earlyVal){console.log(`lateVal is bigger than earlyVal`)};
	if(earlyVal>lateVal){console.log(`earlyVal is bigger than lateVal`)};

	// debug();



</script>

let ID;
const getGistMaxPageNum = () =>{
  const gistCountNumber = Number( document.querySelector("#gistCount").value );
  const maxPageNum = gistCountNumber<10 ? 1 : Math.floor(gistCountNumber /10) + 1;
  return maxPageNum;
}
const changeQuery = () =>{
	ID = document.querySelector("#ID").value;
	document.querySelector("#textField1").value = `seq ${getGistMaxPageNum()}|xargs -P3 -n1 -INUM curl "https://gist.github.com/${ID}?page="NUM >> ./allgist.html`
}

<div class="text-center card-body" id="chronoExample">
Initial: <input type="number" name="number1" id="number1" value="1" min="0" max="1000" onChange="calc()">
Rate: <input type="number" name="number2" id="number2" value="1.2" min="0" max="1000" onChange="calc()">
Times: <input type="number" name="number3" id="number3" value="10" min="0" max="1000" onChange="calc()">
<!-- <input type="button" name="number4" id="number4" value="reverse" onclick="if(reverse){reverse=0}else{reverse=1};calc();" style="width: 100px;height: 100px;"> -->
<a name="number4"  id="number4" value="reverse" onclick="if(reverse){reverse=0}else{reverse=1};calc();" style="padding: 5px 10px;background: #5876a3;">Reverse</a>
<a name="number5"  id="number5" value="decimalPointTruncation" onclick="if(decimalPointTruncation){decimalPointTruncation=0}else{decimalPointTruncation=1};calc();" style="padding: 5px 10px;background: #5876a3;"> Decimal point truncation</a>
<!-- Or less: <input type="number" name="number6" id="number6" value="0" min="0" max="1000" onChange="orLessTaking='1';calc();"> -->
Or less: <input type="number" name="number6" id="number6" min="0" max="1000" onChange="orLessTaking='1';calc();">
Result: <div id="result"></div>
</div>
<script>

	const addHTML = (array) =>{
		const innerArraySetForMakeHTML = (innerArray,KEY) => {
			return `<div class="result"	data-id="${KEY}">
				<span>${innerArray[0]}</span>
				<span>${innerArray[1]}</span>
			</div>`;
		}
		document.querySelector(`#result`).insertAdjacentHTML(`afterBegin`, array.map(innerArraySetForMakeHTML).join(''));
	};

	const deleteHTML = () =>{
		document.querySelectorAll(".result").forEach(E=>{E.parentNode.removeChild(E)});
	}

	// CIC stands for Compound Interest Calculator
	const CIC = (initial,rate,times) =>{
		let resultArray = [];
		let result = initial;
		R.forEach(V=>{
				resultArray.push(result*=rate);
		},R.times(R.identity, times));
		return resultArray
	}
	// CIC(1,1.2,3);// =>[1.2, 1.44, 1.728]

	const orLessTake = (timesArray, CICResultArray) =>{
		// or less 以下
		const orLess = n => n <= parseFloat(document.querySelector("#number6").value);
		// less Than 未満
		// const lessThan = n => n < inputNum;
		CICResultArray = R.takeWhile(orLess, CICResultArray);
		timesArray = R.take(CICResultArray.length , timesArray);
		return [timesArray, CICResultArray];
	}

	let reverse=0;
	let decimalPointTruncation=0;
	let timesArrayAndCICResultArray;
	let orLessTaking;

	const randomRgba = () =>{
		const o = Math.round, r = Math.random, s = 255;
		// return 'rgba(' + o(r()*s) + ',' + o(r()*s) + ',' + o(r()*s) + ',' + r().toFixed(1) + ')';
		return 'rgba(' + o(r()*s) + ',' + o(r()*s) + ',' + o(r()*s) + ',' + 1 + ')';
	}

	let colors=[];
	const makeChart = () =>{
		const ctx = document.getElementById('myChart').getContext('2d');
		colors = R.repeat(null, timesArrayAndCICResultArray.length).map(V=>{return randomRgba()});
		const myChart = new Chart(ctx, {
			type: 'bar',
			data: {
				labels: R.times(R.identity,timesArrayAndCICResultArray.length),
				datasets: [{
					label: 'numbers',
					// data: [12, 19, 3, 5, 2, 3],
					data: R.pluck(1, timesArrayAndCICResultArray),
					// backgroundColor: ['rgba(255, 99, 132, 0.2)', 'rgba(54, 162, 235, 0.2)',
					// 	'rgba(255, 206, 86, 0.2)', 'rgba(75, 192, 192, 0.2)', 'rgba(153, 102, 255, 0.2)',
					// 	'rgba(255, 159, 64, 0.2)'
					// ],
					backgroundColor: colors,
					borderColor: colors,
					borderWidth: 1
				}]
			},
			options: {
				scales: {
					yAxes: [{
						ticks: {
							beginAtZero: true
						}
					}]
				}
			}
		});
	}

	calc = () =>{
		deleteHTML();
		let times = document.querySelector("#number3").value;
		// R.map(n => n + 1, R.times(R.identity, 5)) //=> [1, 2, 3, 4, 5]
		let timesArray = R.map(n => n + 1, R.times(R.identity, times));
		let CICResultArray = CIC(
			document.querySelector("#number1").value,
			document.querySelector("#number2").value,
			document.querySelector("#number3").value
		);

		if(decimalPointTruncation){ CICResultArray = R.map(((E)=>{return [ Math.trunc(E) ]}) , CICResultArray) };
		if(document.querySelector("#number6").value==="0"){orLessTaking=undefined};
		if(orLessTaking){ [timesArray, CICResultArray] = orLessTake(timesArray, CICResultArray) };
		timesArrayAndCICResultArray = R.transpose(
			[
				timesArray, CICResultArray
			]
		)

		if(reverse){timesArrayAndCICResultArray = R.reverse(timesArrayAndCICResultArray)};
		addHTML(timesArrayAndCICResultArray);
		makeChart();
	}


	calc();

</script>

    <script>
		const keyConfig = () => {
			window.addEventListener("keydown", function (event) {
			if (event.defaultPrevented) {
				return; // Do nothing if the event was already processed
			}
				switch (event.key) {
				case "5":
					document.querySelector('#start').click()
				break;
				case "1":
					document.querySelector('#previous').click()
				break;
				case "2":
					document.querySelector('#minibackward').click()
				break;
				case "3":
					document.querySelector('#miniforward').click()
				break;
				case "4":
					document.querySelector('#next').click()
				break;
				case "h":
					document.querySelector('#position').value = 50;
					position();
				break;
				case "Enter":
				default:
				}
			// Cancel the default action to avoid it being handled twice
			event.preventDefault();
			}, true);
		};

        function debugMode(){
            console.log(`videoIndex:${videoIndex}`);
            console.log(`temporaryVolume:${temporaryVolume}`);
            console.log(`document.activeElement.width:${document.activeElement.width}`);
            console.log(`document.activeElement.height:${document.activeElement.height}`);
            console.log(`document.activeElement.currentTime:${document.activeElement.currentTime}`);
        }
        // setInterval(debugMode,10);

//controller--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
        function resize() {
            document.querySelectorAll("video").forEach(video => {
                video.width = (document.querySelector("#resize").value * 160).toString();
                video.height = (document.querySelector("#resize").value * 120).toString();
            })
        }

        let videoIndex = 0;

        function viewSizeZoom() {
            document.activeElement.width *= document.querySelector("#viewSizeZoom").value;
            document.activeElement.height *= document.querySelector("#viewSizeZoom").value;
        }

        function previous() {
            if (videoIndex > 0) {
                resize();
                stop();
                videoIndex--;
                document.querySelectorAll("video")[videoIndex].focus();
                viewSizeZoom();
                document.querySelectorAll("video")[videoIndex].scrollIntoView(true)
                document.activeElement.play();
            };
        }

        function manybackward() {
            document.querySelectorAll("video")[videoIndex].focus();
            document.activeElement.currentTime -= document.activeElement.duration / 5;
        }

        function backward() {
            document.querySelectorAll("video")[videoIndex].focus();
            document.activeElement.currentTime -= document.activeElement.duration / 10;
        }

        function fewbackward() {
            document.querySelectorAll("video")[videoIndex].focus();
            document.activeElement.currentTime -= document.activeElement.duration / 30;
        }

        function minibackward() {
            document.querySelectorAll("video")[videoIndex].focus();
            document.activeElement.currentTime -= document.activeElement.duration / 100;
        }

        function stop() {
            document.querySelectorAll("video").forEach(video => {
                video.pause();
                document.querySelectorAll("video")[videoIndex].focus();
            })
        }
        
        function start(event) {
            resize();
            if(/[0-9]+/.test(event.target.id)){
                videoIndex = event.target.id;
                document.querySelectorAll("video")[videoIndex].focus();
            }else{
                document.querySelectorAll("video")[videoIndex].focus();
            }
            viewSizeZoom();
            document.querySelectorAll("video")[videoIndex].scrollIntoView(true)
            document.activeElement.play();
        }
        document.querySelector("#start").addEventListener("click", start, false);

        function miniforward() {
            document.querySelectorAll("video")[videoIndex].focus();
            document.activeElement.currentTime += document.activeElement.duration / 100;
        }

        function fewforward() {
            document.querySelectorAll("video")[videoIndex].focus();
            document.activeElement.currentTime += document.activeElement.duration / 30;
        }

        function forward() {
            document.querySelectorAll("video")[videoIndex].focus();
            document.activeElement.currentTime += document.activeElement.duration / 10;
        }

        function manyforward() {
            document.querySelectorAll("video")[videoIndex].focus();
            document.activeElement.currentTime += document.activeElement.duration / 5;
        }

        function next() {
            if (videoIndex < document.querySelectorAll("video").length) {
                resize();
                stop();
                if(videoIndex !== document.querySelectorAll("video").length-1){videoIndex++};
                document.querySelectorAll("video")[videoIndex].focus();
                viewSizeZoom();
                document.querySelectorAll("video")[videoIndex].scrollIntoView(true)
                document.activeElement.play();
            }
        }

        function position() {
            document.querySelectorAll("video").forEach(video => {
                video.currentTime = video.duration / 100 * document.querySelector("#position").value;
            })
        }

        function loop() {
            document.querySelectorAll("video").forEach(video => {
                video.loop = document.querySelector("#loop").checked;
            })
        }

        function hoverplayorpause() {
            document.querySelectorAll("video").forEach(video => {
                document.querySelector("#hoverplayorpause").checked ? video.setAttribute("onmouseover","start(event)") : video.removeAttribute("onmouseover");
                document.querySelector("#hoverplayorpause").checked ? video.setAttribute("onmouseout","stop()") : video.removeAttribute("onmouseout");
            })
        }

        function allplayorpause() {
            document.querySelectorAll("video").forEach(video => {
                video.paused ? video.play() : video.pause();
            })
        }


        function volume() {
            document.querySelectorAll("video").forEach(video => {
                video.volume = document.querySelector("#volume").value;
            })
        }

        let temporaryVolume;

        function mute() {
            document.querySelectorAll("video").forEach(video => {
                if (video.volume !== 0) {
                    temporaryVolume = video.volume;
                    video.volume = 0;
                    document.querySelector("#volume").value = 0;
                } else {
                    video.volume = temporaryVolume;
                    document.querySelector("#volume").value = temporaryVolume;
                }
            })
        }
//controller--------------------------------------------------------------------------------







//drop_zone---------------------------------------------------------------------------------
        function appendVideo(filesName) {
            let id = 0;
            for (let fileName of filesName) {
                let video = document.createElement("video");
                video.setAttribute("class", "video1");
                video.setAttribute("controls", false);
                video.setAttribute("width", "160");
                video.setAttribute("height", "120");
                video.setAttribute("id", id);
                id += 1;
                let source = document.createElement("source");
                source.setAttribute("src", fileName);
                video.appendChild(source);
                document.querySelector("body").appendChild(video);
                hoverplayorpause();
            }
        }

		let filesName = [];
        function dropHandler(ev) {
            console.log('File(s) dropped');

            ev.preventDefault();

            // let filesName = [];
            if (ev.dataTransfer.items) {
                for (var i = 0; i < ev.dataTransfer.items.length; i++) {
                    if (ev.dataTransfer.items[i].kind === 'file') {
                        var file = ev.dataTransfer.items[i].getAsFile();
                        // console.log(let hoge = window.URL.createObjectURL(file));
                        // console.log('...file[' + i + '].name = ' + file.name);
                        console.log(file.name);
                        filesName.push(window.URL.createObjectURL(file));
                    }
                }
            } else {
                for (var i = 0; i < ev.dataTransfer.files.length; i++) {
                    console.log('... file[' + i + '].name = ' + ev.dataTransfer.files[i].name);
                }
            }
            appendVideo(filesName);
            filesName = [];
        }

        function dragOverHandler(ev) {
            // console.log('File(s) in drop zone'); // Prevent default behavior (Prevent file from being opened)
            document.querySelector("#drop_zone").style = "border:3px solid gray"
            ev.preventDefault();
        }
//drop_zone---------------------------------------------------------------------------------

    </script>
</body>

<script>
    let canvas = document.getElementById('myCanvas');
    let ctx = canvas.getContext('2d');
    ctx.beginPath();
    ctx.fillStyle = "white";
    ctx.fillRect(0, 0, 1200, 600);

    const shuffleArray = array => {
      for (let i = array.length - 1; i > 0; i--) {
        let r = Math.floor(Math.random() * (i + 1));
        let tmp = array[i];
        array[i] = array[r];
        array[r] = tmp;
      }
      return array
    }

	const randomRange = (from, to) => { return shuffleArray(R.range(from, to)) };

	let V1_0_700_x = randomRange(0, 1200);
	let V1_0_400_y = randomRange(0, 600);
	const fromTo = (fromX,fromY,toX,toY) => {
		ctx.strokeStyle = `rgba( ${Math.floor(Math.random() * (255 + 1))}, ${Math.floor(Math.random() * (255 + 1))} , ${Math.floor(Math.random() * (255 + 1))}, ${Math.floor(Math.random() * (255 + 1))} )`;
		ctx.createLinearGradient(fromX,fromY,toX,toY);
		ctx.lineWidth =  200;
		ctx.globalAlpha = 0.9;
		ctx.lineCap = "round";
		ctx.moveTo(fromX,fromY);
		ctx.lineTo(toX,toY);
		ctx.moveTo(toX,toY);
	}
	fromTo(V1_0_700_x[0],V1_0_400_y[0],V1_0_700_x[1],V1_0_400_y[1]);

	const randomPaint = NUM => fromTo(V1_0_700_x[NUM],V1_0_400_y[NUM],V1_0_700_x[NUM+1],V1_0_400_y[NUM+1]);
	const numberOfLines = (NUM) => { return R.range(1, NUM) };

	const randomDraw = (time) => {
		V1_0_700_x = randomRange(-100, 1200);
		V1_0_400_y = randomRange(-100, 800);
		ctx.beginPath();
		R.forEach(randomPaint, numberOfLines(time) );
		ctx.stroke();
	}

	const draw = () =>{ 
		randomDraw( Math.floor(Math.random() * (50 + 1)));
		randomDraw( Math.floor(Math.random() * (50 + 1)));
		randomDraw( Math.floor(Math.random() * (50 + 1)));
		randomDraw( Math.floor(Math.random() * (50 + 1)));
		randomDraw( Math.floor(Math.random() * (50 + 1)));
		randomDraw( Math.floor(Math.random() * (50 + 1)));
		randomDraw( Math.floor(Math.random() * (50 + 1)));
		randomDraw( Math.floor(Math.random() * (50 + 1)));
		randomDraw( Math.floor(Math.random() * (50 + 1)));
		randomDraw( Math.floor(Math.random() * (50 + 1)));
		randomDraw( Math.floor(Math.random() * (50 + 1)));
	 }

	const getPic = () =>{
		var link = document.getElementById('link');
		link.setAttribute('download', 'foo.jpg');
		link.setAttribute('href', canvas.toDataURL("image/jpeg").replace("image/jpeg", "image/octet-stream"));
		link.click();
	}
</script>

<script>
	new ClipboardJS('.btn');
	let sample;
	const count = ()=>{
		const val0 = R.split(" ")(document.querySelector(`#foo`).value);
		const val1 = R.countBy(R.identity)(val0);
		const val2 = R.toPairs(val1);
		const by1AryDescend = R.descend(R.prop(1));
		const val3 = R.sort(by1AryDescend, val2);
		const UNDER = N => N[1] <= Number(document.querySelector(`#number1`).value);
		const val4 = R.filter(UNDER, val3);
		const OVER = N => N[1] >= Number(document.querySelector(`#number0`).value);
		const val5 = R.filter(OVER, val4);
		document.querySelector(`#bar`).value = R.join("\n")(R.pluck(0)(val5));
		document.querySelector(`#baz`).value = R.join("\n")(R.pluck(1)(val5));
		sample = R.clone(val5);
	}

     async function test() {
        document.querySelector(`#foo`).value = await WethePeopleoftheUnitedStates;
		count();
		console.table(sample);
    }

			<option value="return">return</option>
			<option value="dot">dot</option>
			<option value="comma">comma</option>
			<option value="tab">tab</option>
		</select>
		<textarea name="foo" id="foo" cols="50" rows="10" required="required" autofocus="autofocus" placeholder="foo bar foo baz" onInput="makeList();"></textarea>

<script>
let forConsoleDisplay;
let allText,allEachTag,allTextAndAllEachTag,allTag=[];

const exe = ()=>{
	const separator = document.querySelector("#separator").value;
	switch (separator) {
	case 'return':
		allText = R.split("\n")(document.querySelector(`#foo`).value);
		break;
	case 'dot':
		allText = R.split(".")(document.querySelector(`#foo`).value);
		break;
	case 'comma':
		allText = R.split(",")(document.querySelector(`#foo`).value);
		break;
	case 'tab':
		allText = R.split("\t")(document.querySelector(`#foo`).value);
		break;
	default:
		allText = R.split("\n")(document.querySelector(`#foo`).value);
	};
	allEachTag = R.map(V=>{return R.split(" ",V)},allText);
	allTextAndAllEachTag = R.zip(allText,allEachTag);
	allTag = R.pipe(R.flatten,R.uniq)(allEachTag);
	document.querySelector(`#bar`).value = R.toString(allTextAndAllEachTag);
	forConsoleDisplay = R.clone(allTextAndAllEachTag);
}
const insertText=(event)=>{
	const val0 = R.filter(V=>R.includes(event.target.dataset.text,V[1]))(allTextAndAllEachTag);
	const val1 = R.pluck(0,val0);
	const val2 = R.join("\n")(val1);
	document.querySelector(`#foo1`).value = val2;
}
const makeLiTag = (array) => R.pipe(R.map(V=>{return `<li class="taglist" type="button" value='${V}' data-text='${V}' onclick="insertText(event)">${V}</li>`}), R.join(""))(array);
const addHTML = (htmlstring) =>	document.querySelector(`#tag`).insertAdjacentHTML(`beforeend`, htmlstring);
const makeList = () =>{
		exe();
		console.table(forConsoleDisplay);
		document.querySelectorAll(".taglist").forEach(E=>{E.parentNode.removeChild(E)});
		addHTML(makeLiTag(allTag));
}
// when use develop for test--------------
const test = () =>{
	let test;
	let onlyExeTime=true;
	test=true;
	if(onlyExeTime&&test){
		document.querySelector(`#foo`).value =
`one foo.
two. bar
three, bar hoge.
four foo, baz
five baz,
six, bar baz.`
		onlyExeTime=false;
	}
	makeList();
}
document.querySelector("#test").click();
// when use develop for test--------------

makeList();
</script>
